## rentcafe-houston

# Houston, TX Rental Market Trends

Last updated: February 03, 2026 \| Source: RentCafe Market Analysis, Yardi Matrix, U.S. Census Bureau

## Highlights

The average rent for an apartment in Houston is $1,347, a 0.74% decrease compared to the previous year, when the average rent was $1,357.

Studio Apartments at $1,010 offer the most budget-friendly option with 508 square feet, ideal for single renters prioritizing location over space.

One-bedroom apartments provide 731 square feet for $1,196, balancing privacy and affordability.

Two-beedroom units at $1,510 offer 1,054 square feet, perfect for roommates or small families.

Three-bedroom apartments deliver maximum space (1,368 sq ft) for $1,838, suitable for larger households.

## Average rent in Houston, TX

Last updated: February 03, 2026


|  | Average Rent | Average Apartment Size |
| --- | --- | --- |
| All Rentals | $1,347 | 883 sq. ft. |
| Studio | $1,010 | 508 sq. ft. |
| 1 Bed | $1,196 | 731 sq. ft. |
| 2 Beds | $1,510 | 1,054 sq. ft. |
| 3 Beds | $1,838 | 1,368 sq. ft. |

## Houston, TX rent trends

## What's the typical rent budget in Houston, TX?

The largest share of rentals in Houston, TX (45%) fall between $1,001-$1,500 per month. This suggests that most people succesfully find suitable apartments within this price.

## Do most people rent or own in Houston, TX?

531,864 or 58% of the households in Houston, TX are renter-occupied while 384,672 or 42% are owner-occupied.

Yardi® Matrix

[Learn more](https://www.yardimatrix.com/)

All of these neighborhoods fall below the city wide average of $1,347/month.

[University Place](https://www.rentcafe.com/apartments-for-rent/us/tx/harris-county/houston/university-place/) $2,539/month

These neighborhoods typically command higher rents due to location, amenities, and demand.

## Where this data comes from

The rental statistics on this page were compiled by RentCafe.com, a nationwide apartment search website trusted by millions of renters to find apartments and houses for rent throughout the U.S.

Rent prices, trends, and apartment sizes were calculated based on data from our sister company, Yardi Matrix, an apartment market intelligence solution that covers approximately 90% of the U.S. metro area population. The data includes comprehensive information on all Houston apartment buildings with 50 or more units, totaling 23.5 million apartments across 181 U.S. markets.

Housing composition data was sourced from the U.S. Census Bureau, using the most recently available information by tenure.

## clearlake-rent

# Clear Lake, Houston, TX Rental Market Trends

Last updated: February 03, 2026 \| Source: RentCafe Market Analysis, Yardi Matrix, U.S. Census Bureau

## Highlights

The average rent for an apartment in Clear Lake is $1,232, a 2.65% decrease compared to the previous year, when the average rent was $1,265.

Studio Apartments at $827 offer the most budget-friendly option with 445 square feet, ideal for single renters prioritizing location over space.

One-bedroom apartments provide 724 square feet for $1,078, balancing privacy and affordability.

Two-beedroom units at $1,351 offer 1,025 square feet, perfect for roommates or small families.

Three-bedroom apartments deliver maximum space (1,359 sq ft) for $1,662, suitable for larger households.

## Average rent in Clear Lake, Houston, TX

Last updated: February 03, 2026

| --- | --- | --- |

| Studio | $827 | 445 sq. ft. |
| 1 Bed | $1,078 | 724 sq. ft. |
| 2 Beds | $1,351 | 1,025 sq. ft. |
| 3 Beds | $1,662 | 1,359 sq. ft. |

## Clear Lake, Houston, TX rent trends

Rental prices in Clear Lake, Houston, TX have decreased by 2.65% over the past year. The average rent moved from $1,265 to $1,232.

## What's the typical rent budget in Clear Lake, Houston, TX?

The largest share of rentals in Clear Lake, Houston, TX (53%) fall between $1,001-$1,500 per month. This suggests that most people succesfully find suitable apartments within this price.

## Do most people rent or own in Clear Lake, Houston, TX?

5,908 or 31% of the households in Clear Lake, Houston, TX are renter-occupied while 13,292 or 69% are owner-occupied.

## Where this data comes from

The rental statistics on this page were compiled by RentCafe.com, a nationwide apartment search website trusted by millions of renters to find apartments and houses for rent throughout the U.S.

Rent prices, trends, and apartment sizes were calculated based on data from our sister company, Yardi Matrix, an apartment market intelligence solution that covers approximately 90% of the U.S. metro area population. The data includes comprehensive information on all Clear Lake apartment buildings with 50 or more units, totaling 23.5 million apartments across 181 U.S. markets.

Housing composition data was sourced from the U.S. Census Bureau, using the most recently available information by tenure.

## downtown-rent

# Downtown Houston, Houston, TX Rental Market Trends

Last updated: February 03, 2026 \| Source: RentCafe Market Analysis, Yardi Matrix, U.S. Census Bureau

## Highlights

The average rent for an apartment in Downtown Houston is $2,268, a 5.8% decrease compared to the previous year, when the average rent was $2,408.

Studio Apartments at $1,455 offer the most budget-friendly option with 579 square feet, ideal for single renters prioritizing location over space.

One-bedroom apartments provide 833 square feet for $1,940, balancing privacy and affordability.

Two-beedroom units at $3,212 offer 1,400 square feet, perfect for roommates or small families.

Three-bedroom apartments deliver maximum space (2,318 sq ft) for $5,337, suitable for larger households.

## Average rent in Downtown Houston, Houston, TX

Last updated: February 03, 2026


|  | Average Rent | Average Apartment Size |
| --- | --- | --- |
| All Rentals | $2,268 | 977 sq. ft. |
| Studio | $1,455 | 579 sq. ft. |
| 1 Bed | $1,940 | 833 sq. ft. |
| 2 Beds | $3,212 | 1,400 sq. ft. |
| 3 Beds | $5,337 | 2,318 sq. ft. |

## Downtown Houston, Houston, TX rent trends

Rental prices in Downtown Houston, Houston, TX have decreased by 5.8% over the past year. The average rent moved from $2,408 to $2,268.

## What's the typical rent budget in Downtown Houston, Houston, TX?

The largest share of rentals in Downtown Houston, Houston, TX (37%) fall between $1,501-$2,000 per month. This suggests that most people succesfully find suitable apartments within this price.

## Do most people rent or own in Downtown Houston, Houston, TX?

6,100 or 83% of the households in Downtown Houston, Houston, TX are renter-occupied while 1,264 or 17% are owner-occupied.

Yardi® Matrix

[Learn more](https://www.yardimatrix.com/)

[Woodglen Village](https://www.rentcafe.com/apartments-for-rent/us/tx/houston/woodglen-village/) $965/month

All of these neighborhoods fall below the city wide average of $1,347/month.

## Where this data comes from

The rental statistics on this page were compiled by RentCafe.com, a nationwide apartment search website trusted by millions of renters to find apartments and houses for rent throughout the U.S.

Rent prices, trends, and apartment sizes were calculated based on data from our sister company, Yardi Matrix, an apartment market intelligence solution that covers approximately 90% of the U.S. metro area population. The data includes comprehensive information on all Medical Center apartment buildings with 50 or more units, totaling 23.5 million apartments across 181 U.S. markets.

Housing composition data was sourced from the U.S. Census Bureau, using the most recently available information by tenure.

## memorial-rent

# Memorial, Houston, TX Rental Market Trends

Last updated: February 03, 2026 \| Source: RentCafe Market Analysis, Yardi Matrix, U.S. Census Bureau

## Highlights

The average rent for an apartment in Memorial is $2,107, a 0.52% increase compared to the previous year, when the average rent was $2,096.

Studio Apartments at $1,494 offer the most budget-friendly option with 607 square feet, ideal for single renters prioritizing location over space.

One-bedroom apartments provide 789 square feet for $1,750, balancing privacy and affordability.

Two-beedroom units at $2,616 offer 1,258 square feet, perfect for roommates or small families.

Three-bedroom apartments deliver maximum space (1,796 sq ft) for $3,742, suitable for larger households.

## Average rent in Memorial, Houston, TX

Last updated: February 03, 2026


|  | Average Rent | Average Apartment Size |
| --- | --- | --- |
| All Rentals | $2,107 | 979 sq. ft. |
| Studio | $1,494 | 607 sq. ft. |
| 1 Bed | $1,750 | 789 sq. ft. |
| 2 Beds | $2,616 | 1,258 sq. ft. |
| 3 Beds | $3,742 | 1,796 sq. ft. |

## Memorial, Houston, TX rent trends

Rental prices in Memorial, Houston, TX have increased by 0.52% over the past year. The average rent moved from $2,096 to $2,107.

## What's the typical rent budget in Memorial, Houston, TX?

The largest share of rentals in Memorial, Houston, TX (39%) fall between $1,501-$2,000 per month. This suggests that most people succesfully find suitable apartments within this price.

## Do most people rent or own in Memorial, Houston, TX?

3,728 or 43% of the households in Memorial, Houston, TX are renter-occupied while 4,876 or 57% are owner-occupied.

Two-beedroom units at $2,142 offer 1,232 square feet, perfect for roommates or small families.

## Where this data comes from

The rental statistics on this page were compiled by RentCafe.com, a nationwide apartment search website trusted by millions of renters to find apartments and houses for rent throughout the U.S.

Rent prices, trends, and apartment sizes were calculated based on data from our sister company, Yardi Matrix, an apartment market intelligence solution that covers approximately 90% of the U.S. metro area population. The data includes comprehensive information on all Midtown Houston apartment buildings with 50 or more units, totaling 23.5 million apartments across 181 U.S. markets.

Housing composition data was sourced from the U.S. Census Bureau, using the most recently available information by tenure.

## Houston, TX market summary

Reporting period: December 2025

![Map of Houston](data:image/svg+xml,%3Csvg xmlns='http://www.w3.org/2000/svg'/%3E)

Search homes & rentals in Houston

[Search 15.7K homes](https://www.realtor.com/realestateandhomes-search/Houston_TX) [Search 13.8K rentals](https://www.realtor.com/apartments/Houston_TX)

| Metric | Citywide | 1Y Change | 3Y Change |
| --- | --- | --- | --- |
| Median home $ | $316,000 | -3.36% | -8.38% |
| $ per sq ft | $169/sq ft | -2.87% | -5.06% |
| Active listings | 15,653 | 14.32% | 51.48% |
| Avg days on market | 68 days | 11.48% | 28.30% |
| Rental properties | 13,834 | -41.14% | -4.45% |
| Median rent | $1,769/mo | 7.02% | 6.57% |

Source: Realtor.com® Economic Research — our Residential Real Estate Data Library integrates the extensive [Realtor.com](https://www.realtor.com/) database of MLS-listed for-sale homes with proprietary metrics and advanced econometrics to deliver a precise, timely view of housing trends.


The data points on this page are chosen to give buyers, sellers, and renters the most actionable insights. Buyers can gauge price **trends and inventory** to time their purchase. Sellers get clarity on **demand, pricing power, and days on market**. Renters see how current **costs are shifting across areas**. Together, these metrics offer a **clear snapshot** of the housing landscape and help users make more **confident decisions**.

Houston’s median home sale price is **$316,000**, signaling balanced pricing for buyers and sellers. The for-sale market shows a year-over-year change in days on market of **11.48%**. The median rental price is **$1,769** per month, and the price per square foot is **$169**, providing additional context for buyers and investors.

### Houston Quick Market Insights

- **Sales Momentum:** Year-over-year home sale prices softened by **-3.36%**, affecting negotiation dynamics for buyers and sellers.
- **Rentals Demand:** The median rent remains **$1,769** per month, underscoring ongoing demand from renters and favorable conditions for landlords.
- **Inventory And Supply:** Active for-sale listings total **15.7K**, reflecting a sizable inventory that informs bidding strategy.
- **Price Density:** The price per square foot sits at **$169**, highlighting neighborhood valuation differences and helping buyers compare options.

## For buyers

Houston buyers can start with about **15.7K** homes for sale, a median list price of **$316,000**, and a median of **68** days on market. Year-over-year, the for-sale count has risen by **14.32%**, the for-sale price median has fallen by **-3.36%**, the for-sale days on market median has increased by **11.48%**, and the price per square foot has declined by **-2.87%**. Month-over-month, the for-sale count has fallen by **-6.36%**, the for-sale price median has fallen by **-1.25%**, and the for-sale days on market median has increased by **19.30%**.

## FAQs for buyers in Houston, TX

### How affordable is it to live in Houston?

Buyers should run a personalized affordability check using income, debt, and down payment assumptions. Then use the [Affordability Calculator](https://www.realtor.com/mortgage/tools/affordability-calculator/) to estimate monthly costs.

### What should new buyers know about Houston’s real estate landscape?

Houston offers diverse neighborhoods with varying price ranges, amenities, and styles, making research and planning essential. A good starting point is reviewing neighborhood insights, school options, and market context provided by realtor.com.

### What are the current listing statistics in Houston?

The median listing price is **$316,000** and there are **15,653** homes for sale. The median price per square foot is **$169**.

### How did month-over-month performance change in Houston?

Month-over-month, for-sale count declined by **-6.36%** and the median price per square foot fell by **-0.59%**. Days on market rose by **19.3%**.

### How did year-over-year metrics look in Houston?

Year-over-year, for-sale count rose by **14.32%** and the price per square foot declined by **-2.87%**. Days on market increased year-over-year by **11.48%**.

### What are the three-year trends for Houston’s listings?

Over three years, the for-sale count increased by **51.48%** and the three-year median price per listing changed by **-8.38%**. The three-year days on market median rose by **28.3%**.

## For sellers

The Houston seller market shows resilient demand with a steady inventory profile and pricing discipline that can support confident listings. Despite fluctuations, the market indicates buyers remain motivated to close at or near asking prices, underscored by a high sales-to-list-price ratio and a steady days-on-market baseline. Year-over-year trends point to growing listing activity while price momentum remains cautious, suggesting strategic timing and pricing remain key opportunities for sellers. The Houston market’s median listing price is **$316,000**, and about **15.7K** homes are listed for sale. Month-over-month metrics show the for-sale count at **-6.36%**, the median price at **-1.25%**, the days-on-market at **19.30%** higher, and the price per square foot at **-0.59%**. Year-over-year, for-sale count rose by **14.32%**, while the median sale price declined by **-3.36%**, days on market moved up by **11.48%**, and price per square foot fell by **-2.87%**.

- [Inner Loop](https://www.realtor.com/local/market/texas/houston/inner-loop "Inner Loop"): **$539,000** Median Home Price \| **69** Avg. Days On Market
- [Westside](https://www.realtor.com/local/market/texas/houston/westside "Westside"): **$271,500** Median Home Price \| **72** Avg. Days On Market
- [North Houston](https://www.realtor.com/local/market/texas/houston/north-houston "North Houston"): **$339,900** Median Home Price \| **64** Avg. Days On Market
- [Northeast Houston](https://www.realtor.com/local/market/texas/houston/northeast-houston "Northeast Houston"): **$229,990** Median Home Price \| **68** Avg. Days On Market

- [77091](https://www.realtor.com/local/market/texas/zipcode-77091 "77091"): **$339,900** Median Home Price \| **62** Avg. Days On Market

## For renters

Houston’s rental landscape offers a sizable market for rentals, featuring dynamic demand and a broad range of options that create opportunities for flexible, affordable living. In Houston, the median rent is **$1,769** and there are **13.8K** rentals available. Month-over-month, the rentals count declined by **-22.23%** and the median rent changed by **-0.23%**. Year-over-year, the rentals count fell by **-41.14%** and the year-over-year median rent rose by **7.02%**.

- [Inner Loop](https://www.realtor.com/local/market/texas/houston/inner-loop "Inner Loop"): **$1,881** Median Rent \| **2,916** Rentals

## redfin-houston-market

# Houston, TX Housing Market

[Homes for sale](https://www.redfin.com/city/8903/TX/Houston) \| [City guide](https://www.redfin.com/living-in/TX/Houston/6/8903)

The Houston housing market is somewhat competitive. Homes in Houston receive 1 offers on average and sell in around 70 days. The median sale price of a home in Houston was $335K last month, down 5.4% since last year. The median sale price per square foot in Houston is $171, down 1.2% since last year.

- [Trends](https://www.redfin.com/city/8903/TX/Houston/housing-market#trends)

- [Transportation](https://www.redfin.com/city/8903/TX/Houston/housing-market#transportation)

## Houston Housing Market Trends

What is the housing market like in Houston today?

In December 2025, Houston home prices were down 5.4% compared to last year, selling for a median price of $335K. On average, homes in Houston sell after 70 days on the market compared to 50 days last year. There were 1,632 homes sold in December this year, up from 1,580 last year.

## Houston Migration & Relocation Trends

In Oct '25 -Dec '25, 37% ofHouston homebuyers searched to move out of Houston, while63% looked to stay within the metropolitan area.

Where are people moving to Houston from?

- Across the nation, 1% of homebuyers searched to move into Houston from outside metros.
- St. Louis homebuyers searched to move into Houston more than any other metro followed byLos Angeles andWashington.

Where are people from Houston moving to?

- 63% of Houston homebuyers searched to stay within the Houston metropolitan area.
- Sacramento was the most popular destination among Houston homebuyers followed bySeattle andAustin.

Methodology

This data does not reflect actual moves. The latest migration analysis is based on a sample of about two
million Redfin.com users who searched for homes across more than 100 metro areas. To be included in this dataset, a Redfin.com user
must have viewed at least 10 homes in a three month period. This dataset excludes all rentals data.

## Climate's impact on Houston housing

Learn about natural hazards and environmental risks, such as floods, fires, wind, and heat that
could impact homes in Houston.

### Flood Factor \- Major

60% of properties are at risk of severe flooding over the next 30 years

* * *

### Flood Factor

![flood factor score logo](https://ssl.cdn-redfin.com/vLATEST/images/riskFactor/regional/flood-3.png)

Houston has a major risk of flooding. 181,932 propertiesin Houston are likely to be

severely affected

by flooding over the next 30 years. This represents 60% of all properties in Houston. Flood risk is increasing slower than the national average.

[Learn more on First Street™](https://firststreet.org/city/houston-tx/4835000_fsid/flood?utm_source=redfin)

### Fire Factor \- Moderate

20% of properties are at risk of wildfire over the next 30 years

* * *

### Fire Factor

![fire factor score logo](https://ssl.cdn-redfin.com/vLATEST/images/riskFactor/regional/fire-2.png)

Houston has a moderaterisk of wildfire. There are 126,236 properties in Houston that have some risk of being affected by wildfire over the next 30 years. This represents 20% of all properties in Houston.

[Learn more on First Street™](https://firststreet.org/city/houston-tx/4835000_fsid/fire?utm_source=redfin)

### Wind Factor \- Extreme

96% of properties are at extreme
risk of a severe wind event over the next 30 years

* * *

### Wind Factor

![wind factor score logo](https://ssl.cdn-redfin.com/vLATEST/images/riskFactor/regional/wind-5.png)

Houston has an Extreme Wind Factor® risk based on the projected likelihood and speed of hurricane, tornado, or severe storm winds impacting it. Houstonis most at risk from hurricanes. 589,638 properties in Houston have some risk of being in a severe wind event within the next 30 years.

### Wind likelihood over time

If an exceedingly rare windstorm

(a 1-in-3,000 year storm event)

occurred today, it could cause wind gusts of up to 216 mph. In 30 years, an event of this same likelihood would show increased wind gusts of up to 230 mph.

[Learn more on First Street™](https://firststreet.org/city/houston-tx/4835000_fsid/wind?utm_source=redfin)

### Heat Factor \- Extreme

98% of properties are at extreme
risk of heat over the next 30 years

* * *

### Heat Factor

![heat factor score logo](https://ssl.cdn-redfin.com/vLATEST/images/riskFactor/regional/heat-5.png)

Houston has an extremerisk from heat. This is due to

"feels like" temperatures

increasing, and because 98% of homes in Houston havean Extreme Heat Factor®.

Houston is expected to see a 228%increase in the number of days over 110ºF over the next 30 years. Houston is expected to experience 6

hot days

this year, and23 days above 110ºF in 30 years.

[Learn more on First Street™](https://firststreet.org/city/houston-tx/4835000_fsid/heat?utm_source=redfin)

Provided by First Street Foundation

# Houston, TX Housing Market

## $260,121

**3.0% 1-yr**

The average Houston, TX home value is $260,121, down 3.0% over the past year and goes to pending in around 50 days.

### What is the Zillow Home Values Index?

Zillow Home Value Index (ZHVI), built from the ground up by measuring monthly changes in property level Zestimates, captures both the level and home values across a wide variety of geographies and housing types.

[Learn more about the Zillow Home Value Index](https://www.zillow.com/research/zhvi-methodology-2019-highlights-26221/)

**How does this data help me?**

Zillow's metrics provide valuable market data by tracking market changes in different locations and housing types.

**How does this data help me?**

The Zillow Observed Rent Index (ZORI) measures changes in asking rents over time, controlling for changes in the quality of the available rental inventory.
